## Contexts in which the word **discrimination** was used in the Senate during the 1970s

* As the General Assembly of the United Nations has designated 1971 as the International Year for Action to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> will the Government make an early statement on whether it will actively support this decision, which would be in line with Australia's subscription to the Universal Declaration of Human Rights? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1970/19700521_senate_27_s44/#subdebate-10-0)

* I believe that there is justice in this recommendation and that there is unfair <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against the people of Queensland. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1970/19700602_senate_27_s44/#debate-56)

* Government in the Senate aware that hundreds of thousands of workers throughout Australia today stopped work and that workers and pensioners attended mass rallies protesting at the injustices and economic <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> of the Budget? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1970/19700825_senate_27_s45/#subdebate-0-0)

* I think it should be clearly emphasised that it cannot be charged against the Government that it practises <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in its policy towards Aboriginals in the Northern Territory. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1971/19710331_senate_27_s47/#subdebate-6-0)

* In view of the fact that other handicapped persons who have sight can sit for such examinations will the Minister see to what extent special facilities can be made available to avoid any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against people without sight? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1971/19710514_senate_27_s48/#subdebate-4-0)

* The next is: 'The avoidance of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on any grounds of race or colour of skin or nationality'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1971/19711202_senate_27_s50/#subdebate-39-0)

* Was  Mr Ivica  Kokic ever in charge of the Commonwealth Employment Office in Sunshine; if so, was he transferred to Melbourne due to his <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against non-Croat Yugoslav migrants. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1972/19720524_senate_27_s52/#subdebate-66-0)

* If the Minister considers the situation is unfair to the patients of optometrists, will he take acion to remove this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1972/19720829_senate_27_s53/#subdebate-49-0)

* If so what is the reason for this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19730918_senate_28_s57/#subdebate-52-4)

* Do any laws of the Commonwealth, in any way, contain elements of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731127_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-32-0)

* But its big inconsistency is its <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731205_senate_28_s58/#debate-57)

* That leave bc given to introduce a Bill for an Act relating to the Elimination of Racial and Other <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740403_senate_28_s59/#debate-1)

* Stop the Government practice of trade union membership <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740408_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-0-0)

* They all add up to one thing: <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> at the expense of the black people of my State. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740711_senate_29_s60/#subdebate-47-0)

* Will the Minister ask his colleague to inform the Senate on what basis this unfair <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is being enforced? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740718_senate_29_s60/#subdebate-1-0)

* Will the Government have discussions with the Czechoslovakian Government to abolish this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and to protect the rights of these Australian citizens? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740723_senate_29_s60/#subdebate-5-0)

* That leave be granted to introduce a Bill for an Act relating to the elimination of racial and other <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741022_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-1-1)

* It is racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in its worst form when an Aboriginal senator is discriminated against to that extent. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* Again, that is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by his own parliamentary party. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* I think it is hypocritical for Australia to take such a stand when there is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and prejudice against the indigenous people of this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* You are not allowed to engage in price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731024_senate_28_s57/#subdebate-55-0)

* For example it is an exemption which does not apply to monopolisation, to resale price maintenance, to price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, to this totally new area of consumer protection or to any contracts or combinations having- and these words are so tremendously significant- the purpose or the effect of fixing, controlling or maintaining prices. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731024_senate_28_s57/#subdebate-55-0)

* It deals with such important and significant matters as mergers, monopolisation, exclusive dealing, resale price maintenance and price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731024_senate_28_s57/#subdebate-55-0)

* Given the problems that beset the Builders Labourers Federation official Jack Mundey at the moment, could the Opposition's proposal not be open to <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731025_senate_28_s57/#debate-48)

* I think it could be said that the fact that there is such a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is highly undesirable. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731106_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-52-0)

* As this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is implicitly embodied in this legislation it is a matter of grave concern to the Senate that we should perpetuate such a system. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731106_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-52-0)

* Yet implicit in this legislation is an attempt to perpetuate what is a very gross <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731106_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-52-0)

* This is a principle that provides just terms without <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> for whatever interest you have in land or however large may be your value. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731106_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-52-0)

* -Exactly, and for the litigant whose right of action is taken away by a special piece of legislation the conscience has screwed itself to give itself a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>: It may recompense costs that have been thrown away and, having been thrown away, have become abortive, having regard to the enactment of this Act, when the litigation or arbitration is halfway through its course. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731106_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-52-0)

* This is not in our view any sort of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> based on religious or any other prejudices. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731107_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Anybody who analyses the distribution of the school population between government and non-government schools, I suggest in all sincerity, cannot complain that there is any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> implicit in those figures against non-government schools. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731107_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Will the Minister reconsider the withdrawal of the $3 special compensation allowance which appears as unfair <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against these men and their families? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731108_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-6-0)

* If the Commission provides diversity, freedom of choice and absence of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, its influence will certainly be good. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731113_senate_28_s58/#debate-54)

* In 1970, in the Third Committee of the U.N. General Assembly, the Australian representative expressed concern about the treatment of Jews in the Soviet Union and appealed to the Soviet Union to resist from policies or practices of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against citizens of Jewish origin and to allow those wishing to emigrate to do so. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731113_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-59-6)

* But we have this Government parading Bills of Rights which proclaim that there shall be no <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> between sexes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731114_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-48-0)

* But the idiocy of limiting this compensation to an arbitrary limit of $1,500, assuming a 5,000-bushel crop, is revealed by this attempt to spawn <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> between people who are engaged in a joint association in producing and marketing a crop. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731114_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-48-0)

* We should not accept regional <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> for or against particular regions within States any more than the Constitution allows us to accept <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as between States. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731120_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Bill also provides that everyone is entitled without any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to the equal protection of the law. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill also deals, in clause 15 (2) with the right of women to hold public office on equal terms with men, without <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-39-0)

* This Bill proposes that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> should be made unlawful in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The Universal Declaration proclaims in its first Article that all human beings are born free and equal in dignity and rights and Article 2 provides that everyone is entitled to all the rights and freedoms set out in the Declaration, without distinction of any kind, including <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on grounds of race, colour or national origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> was adopted by the United Nations in 1965. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The United Nations has placed high priority on the advancement of measures for the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in its human rights program. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* A good deal of attention was given to various aspects of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> at the 1968 Teheran Conference on Human Rights held during the International Year for Human Rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The Proclamation of Teheran observed that the implementation of the principle of nondiscrimination, embodied in the United Nations Charter, the Universal Declaration and other international instruments, constituted a most urgent task of mankind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Subsequently, the General Assembly of the United Nations approved a program for the observance of 1 97 1 as the International Year for Action to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The vigorous action initiated by the United Nations in 1971 was followed up in November 1972 by a resolution of the General Assembly in which it was decided to launch a Decade for Action to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> and to inaugurate these activities on 10 December 1973. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Initiative was taken in 1971 by the United Nations Association of Australia which set up a Committee to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The Committee also made representations to the Australian and State governments for the establishment of Race Relations Boards to administer legislation which would prohibit <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on grounds of race in respect of the provision or sale of goods, facilities or services, employment and conditions of employment, membership of trade unions and similar organisations, the purchase, sale or rental of housing accommodation, and the availability of business premises. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The volumes edited by  Mr F.  S. Stevens constitute a valuable contribution to the study of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The volumes on Australian racism disclose various aspects of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> has had its effects on migrant groups in our community and there has been evidence of support in Australia for white racist regimes of South Africa. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Perhaps the most blatant example of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia is that which affects Aboriginals. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> affects Aborigines so far as it concerns the administration of the criminal law and the enjoyment of civil, political, social and economic rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The view is sometimes put that equality is an overriding value and all <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, whether for or against a group is necessarily bad. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* For the past 180 years Aboriginals have suffered enormous handicaps in Australian society by comparison with whites, commencing with violent dispossession from their land and destruction of their social fabric, and continuing through various forms of legal, social and economic <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> does, in fact, recognise the need to take special and concrete measures to ensure the adequate development of certain racial groups for the purpose of guaranteeing them the full and equal enjoyment of human rights and fundamental freedoms, and the Bill gives recognition to this need. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The basic scheme of the Bill is to condemn racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as being unlawful and to provide machinery for investigation and conciliation as well as legal sanctions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The proscribing of acts of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> will have an important persuasive and educative effect. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The fact that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is unlawful will make it easier for people to resist social pressures that result in <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The Bill is divided into 7 parts, the first dealing with preliminary matters, the second with the prohibition of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, the third with investigations and civil proceedings, the fourth with offences, the fifth with the Race Relations Council, the sixth dealing with administrative provisions and the seventh with miscellaneous matters. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Part II of the Bill deals with the prohibition of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* This provision follows closely the definition 'racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>' in the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The purpose of clause 9 is to guarantee equality before the law without <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as to race in the enjoyment of rights and this clause will supersede laws of Australia or of the States that discriminate on grounds of race in relation to the enjoyment of rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Clauses 10 to 15 deal in greater detail with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the enjoyment of rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Clause 10 deals with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> so far as it concerns access to places and facilities, clause 1 1 with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the provision of land, housing and other accommodation and clause 12 with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the provision of goods and services. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* Clause 14 deals with the important aspect of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in employment and clause 15 deals with the display of advertisements that indicate an intention to do an act that is unlawful by reason of the legislation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* There are also offences relating to incitement of racial disharmony, the dissemination of ideas based on racial superiority or hatred with intent to promote hostility or ill will and the incitement of acts of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* This Bill is a first, but essential, step in providing measures for the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia and for the guarantee of rights without <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on grounds of race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* To be effective, however, anti-<span class="highlight">discrimination</span> laws cannot operate in a vacuum. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* I hope that this Bill will not only provide the machinery to deal with acts of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> but also will promote public awareness of this problem which will be so important in achieving the objectives of this legislation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1973/19731121_senate_28_s58/#subdebate-40-0)

* The standards obtained in the development of our society have been achieved without racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and without the problems that have beset other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740319_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-57-0)

* I will take up the matter with the Minister to ascertain the attitude of the Government in regard to air fares and to see whether there has been any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against Western Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740402_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-15-0)

* It is not an area of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against the Commonwealth, nor is it an area of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against Federal law. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740402_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* He revealed the intimidation and the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> practised by Federation Insurance Limited against one of its employees who is a member of the Australian Labor Party. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740402_senate_28_s59/#debate-48)

* Stop the Government practice of trade union membership <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740403_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-0-4)

* This Bill re-introduces, with improvements, the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill 1973, which was introduced into the Senate on 21 November 1973. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The purpose of the Bill is to make racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unlawful in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* It implements into Australian law the obligations contained in the International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The Bill will make it unlawful for a person to do an act involving <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> based on race, colour, descent or national or ethnic origin which impairs the enjoyment of fundamental rights and freedoms. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The Bill guarantees equality before the law without <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> based on race or national origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The Bill goes on to deal in greater detail with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the enjoyment of rights on grounds of race, colour or national or ethnic origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* It deals with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> so far as it concerns access to places and facilities, the provision of land, housing and other accommodation, the provision of goods and services, the right to join trade unions and employment. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* As was the case with the 1973 Bill, machinery to enforce the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> forms an important part of the legislation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* A Race Relations Council will be established to make recommendations on the action that should be taken to bring about the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* In the first place, the Bill has been extended to deal with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against persons on the ground that they are immigrants. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The previous Bill applied only to <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that is made on the grounds of race, colour, descent or national or ethnic origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* This is the basis on which most <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is made against migrant people and the form of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> dealt with by the Convention against Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* However, I have decided that it would be desirable for the Bill to deal also with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> made against a person purely on the ground that he is an immigrant, and the Bill has been so extended. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The Council's role will encompass the areas of educational programs, the promotion of studies and research programs, the publication and dissemination of material to assist in the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and the promotion of understanding, tolerance and friendship among racial or ethnic groups. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

* The changing of community attitudes and the promotion of understanding, tolerance and friendship among racial or ethnic groups will form an extremely important part of the Government 's program for the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740404_senate_28_s59/#subdebate-42-0)

[[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* That is the general prohibition on price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>-  does not apply in relation to a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> if- [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> makes only reasonable allowance for differences in the cost or likely cost of manufacture, distribution, sale or delivery resulting from the differing places to which, methods by which or quantities in which the goods are supplied to the purchasers; or [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is constituted by the doing of an act in good faith to meet a price or benefit offered by a competitor. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* This will mean that the sub-clause will not apply if the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> alleged 'is constituted by the doing of an act in good faith to meet a price or benefit reasonably believed to be offered by a competitor of the supplier'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* The supplier might reasonably respond by saying: 'Yes, but I have this price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> provision and I cannot give you any discount or allowance'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* Is the supplier engaging in the offence of price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> under clause 49? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* Obviously he is offering a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because everyone else is charged $ 1 for the product item but he is offering this customer a price of 95c. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* This supplier is excused from any offence if he can fit himself within the provision to which I am referring; namely, sub-clause ( 1)- the offence of price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>- does not apply in relation to a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> if 'the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is constituted by the doing of an act in good faith to meet a price or benefit offered by a competitor of the supplier'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* We would provide that the person would escape the net in this clause although there was <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* Where <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> has been carried out the person could answer. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* In other words, there is no basis in fact which would justify the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* Immediately those who are practising the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, those who are carrying out the kinds of conduct which are aimed at by this Bill, will have their batteries of lawyers looking into how they can escape the provisions of the legislation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* One is price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* In any proceeding for a contravention  or  sub-section ( I ), the onus of establishing that that sub-section does not apply in relation to a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by reason of sub-section (2) is on the party asserting that sub-section ( 1 ) does not so apply. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* If he has that proof, if he has some satisfactory reason and if he can discharge the onus, the words which  Senator Greenwood  suggests should be added to the clause are desirable and fair, bearing in mind particularly the high penalty which people will pay if convicted of price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* The things that are referred to in this part are contracts and arrangements in restraint of trade, monopolisation, exclusive dealing, price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and mergers. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* The attempt of the draftsman is to incorporate in those 7 paragraphs the matters which it is felt ought not to be taken into account in deciding, for example, whether there has been a contract, arrangement or understanding entered into in restraint of trade or whether there has been exclusive dealing or price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and so on. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740814_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-30-0)

* The Human Rights Bill and the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill which will be introduced into the Parliament by the Government will, when passed, reinforce Australia's compliance with the terms of the genocide convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-15-0)

* I refer now to another example of what we did last night- clause 49 which relates to price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* Not only that, the Committee left it as a matter of fact to be established as to whether there was <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> between purchasers of goods. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* In any proceeding for a contravention of sub-section ( 1 ), the onus of establishing that that sub-section does not apply in relation to a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by reason of sub-section (2) is on the party asserting that sub-section ( 1 ) does not so apply. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* If a competitor is injured by virtue of monopolisation, exclusive dealing or price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, he has a cause of action which he can take to the court. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* But we believe that authorisations should be able to be obtained in respect of monopolisation and price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* If a company can apply to the Commission for an authorisation to engage in conduct which would otherwise be prohibited by clause 45 as being in restraint of trade, or if a company can apply to the Commission for an authorisation to engage in conduct which would otherwise be regarded as exclusive dealing, it seems that there is no proper case for price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and monopolisation not to be able to be excluded. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* I suggest for consideration by the Attorney-General  (Senator Murphy)  that the very width of what is described as monopolisation and price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and the element of uncertainty which must attach to words which are coming into application for the first time in this country warrant the opportunity being given for authorisation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* We do have a basic problem with regard to authorisations, but with regard to monopolisation and price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> one cannot apply for any authorisation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* I simply say that they repeat with regard to conduct which is called price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> the same considerations which we advanced with regard to the other provisions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* We sought to apply that provision now in regard to price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* A private individual suing a company which he alleges has engaged in the practice of monopolisation, price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> or exclusive dealing or which has entered into a contract in restraint of trade under which that individual has suffered loss, could subpoena a member of the Commission to produce all documents relating to the hearing which was then in question. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740815_senate_29_s61/#debate-36)

* I have refered to the Parliamentary Counsel the question of whether we can introduce legislation to overcome <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Queensland. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740816_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-22-0)

* To my mind, the present situation is well within the ambit of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19740816_senate_29_s61/#subdebate-22-0)

* May I interrupt my reading to say that I do not remember hearing any great criticism from our Minister for Foreign Affairs of the day when President Amin took some of his racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to heart and proceeded to act in a reverse way. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* It would be just as easy to ignore the official pronouncements of the Australian Government and to focus exclusively on the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which the white Australians practise against the black Australians. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* I applaud him for his attitude towards and his condemnation of the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which has existed in Australia, but he says that because it exists here, because we are guilty, because we are rotten, low-down and contemptible for tolerating it, we should do nothing to cut it out anywhere else in the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

[[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* Labor's policy on Aboriginal affairs is the only hope we have in Australia of stopping <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* Let us remember that the things that  Senator Webster  hates about <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia and the things that  Senator Coleman  dislikes about Western Australian legislation are hated by all free men and all democrats. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* There is no real movement in sport in South Africa because at the club level where sport starts, not necessarily at the international level, there is still segregation and <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* The honourable senator acknowledged in turn that the reason that we should vote against South Africa is that we have not clean hands on the question of social <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* How can we in Australia say that we are trying to get rid of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and that we believe we should not judge one another because of the colour of our skins, yet turn round and vote the other way when it conies to South Africa? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* We are passing laws and establishing departments to assist and uplift and to get away from racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741029_senate_29_s62/#debate-41)

* The honourable senator referred to the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which is practised against the women senators. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-5-0)

* I do not think that any honourable senator would want to practice any form of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against senators of the other sex. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-5-0)

* I should remind the Senate that although the prohibition of price fixing, monopolisation and anti-competitive mergers in the consumer protection provisions has been operating as from 1 October, the provisions in relation to the prohibition of exclusive dealing, prices <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and contracts in restraint of trade, other than price fixing, are not operative until 1 February 1975. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-29-0)

* The purpose of this Bill is to make racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unlawful in Australia and to provide an effective means of combating racial prejudice in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* I introduced into the Senate a Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill on 21 November 1 973, and again on 4 April 1 974, but the Bill was not debated before Parliament was dissolved for the last election. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill implements into Australian law the obligations contained in the International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill recognises the importance of legislation that will make racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unlawful. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* I emphasise that the introduction of legislation to outlaw racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is a fundamental step that must be taken if Australia is to ratify the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The common law provides no effective remedies against <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the exercise of human rights, whether it be based on race or colour or on other grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* Legislation therefore has a vital role to play in the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The proscribing of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in legislative form not only makes people more aware of the evils of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and makes it more obvious and conspicuous, but also furnishes an essential legal background on which to base changes to basic community attitudes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The fact that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is unlawful will make it easier for people to resist social pressures that result in <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* In making racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unlawful, the Bill follows closely the definition used in the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill will thus make it unlawful for a person to do an act involving <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> based on race, colour, descent or national or ethnic origin which impairs the enjoyment of fundamental rights and freedoms. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* It also deals in detail with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> so far as it concerns access to places and facilities, the provision of land, housing and other accommodation, the provision of goods and services, the right to join trade unions and employment [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* In addition, the Bill establishes formal administrative machinery for the examination of complaints of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on a systematic basis and for the settlement of complaints by conciliation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill also recognises that an emphasis on mediation and conciliation is a more satisfactory way of tackling individual instances of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and the tensions that are associated with individual disputes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill also recognises the importance of developing programs of education and research and other programs to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and promote understanding, tolerance and friendship among racial and ethnic groups. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Commissioner will have the function of conducting programs of education and research to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, and a Community Relations Council will be established with an advisory role. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* A further change to the previous Bills effected by the present Bill will give the Commissioner the function of carrying out and fostering programs of education and research and other programs to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* Overseas experience has shown that the success of legislation dealing with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> depends very much on the effectiveness of programs of this kind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* In my second reading speech of 4 April 1974, 1 pointed out that the changing of community attitudes and the promotion of understanding, tolerance and friendship among racial and ethnic groups would form an extremely important part of government's program for the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* I also pointed out that both government and community-based programs to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> were necessary. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* Australia will be required by Article 7 of the Convention to conduct programs of this kind to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* Finally, the Bill has been amended to emphasise reliance on civil, rather than criminal, law to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill will provide the basis upon which Australia can comply with the obligations imposed by the Convention on Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The Bill recognises that laws proscribing <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> are vital, but not in themselves sufficient. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The legislation recognises that there must also be effective and systematic enforcement of rights and the promotion of education and research, if the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country is to be achieved in fact as well as in theory. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741031_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-39-0)

* The elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> has been one of the major preoccupations of the international community since the Second World War. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* The declaration and subsequent instruments provide, for example, that all are equal before the law and are entitled without any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to equal protection of the law. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* Everyone has the right to just conditions of work without <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and to protection from forced or compulsory labour. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* The International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> (1965), which was signed on behalf of Australia by the then Minister for External Affairs,  Mr Hasluck,  on 13 October 1966, and to which 81 countries have subscribed, requires countries to prohibit racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in all its forms and to guarantee equality before the law without distinction as to race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* The United Nations has supplemented these instruments with numerous resolutions, conferences and programs designed to promote the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* For example, the Proclamation of Teheran issued by the International Conference on Human Rights in 1968 observed that the implementation of the principle of non-<span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, embodied in the United Nations Charter, the Universal Declaration and other instruments constituted a most urgent task of mankind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* It further stated that gross denials of human rights arising from <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on grounds of race outraged the conscience of mankind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* Subsequently, the United Nations designated 1971 as the International Year for Action to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>, and vigorous programs for the year were conducted throughout the world, including Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* On 6 December 1971, the General Assembly of the United Nations adopted a resolution urging further ratifications of the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Convention and this resolution was carried by 10 1 voting in favourincluding Australia- none against and 5 abstentions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* On 10 December 1973, the Decade for Action to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> was inaugurated by the United Nations. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* The program proposed by the United Nations for action on the national level during the decade includes the introduction of legislation, where appropriate, to prevent racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* Against this background, it has been the conscious policy of both Liberal and Labor governments to eliminate all legislation in Australia that contains elements of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* There is legal <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> still in some Australian States against Aboriginals, but my Government has told those States that those laws repealed by those States within two years, or if they are not, we will move in and repeal them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* He regarded the measure as one for the protection of the Aboriginal people and not one of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>- Hansard 20 April 1971, page 1663. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* In 1971 the United Nations Association of Australia set up an Australian Committee to Combat Racism and Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>, as part ofthe United Nations program for the year that I have mentioned. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1974/19741127_senate_29_s62/#subdebate-41-0)

* In its report of its activities of the year, the Committee stated that during the year it had repeatedly urged the Australian and State Governments to repeal all legislation of a discriminatory nature and to take all necessary steps to ratify the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Convention. * Legislation has a vital role to play in the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and the enactment of this Bill is a fundamental step that must be taken if Australia is to ratify the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The common law provides few effective remedies against <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the exercise of human rights, whether it is based on race or colour or on any other grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The proscribing of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in legislative form will make people more aware of the evils of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and will also make it more obvious and conspicuous. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The fact that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is unlawful will make it easier for people to resist social pressures that result in <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* In making racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unlawful, the Bill follows the definition used in the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The Bill will thus make it unlawful for a person to do an act involving <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> based on race, colour, descent or national or ethnic origin which impairs the enjoyment of fundamental rights and freedoms. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* It also deals in detail with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> so far as it concerns access to places and facilities, the provision of land, housing and other accommodation, the provision of goods and services and the right to join trade unions and employment. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The creation of practical and effective legal remedies against <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is an important objective of the Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* In addition, the Bill establishes formal administrative machinery for the examination of complaints of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on a systematic basis and for the settlement of complaints by conciliation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* It is recognised in the legislation that an emphasis on mediation and conciliation is a more satisfactory way of tackling individual instances of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and the tensions that are associated with individual disputes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The Bill recognises the importance of developing programs of education and research and other programs to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and to promote understanding, tolerance and friendship among racial and ethnic groups. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* Overseas experience has shown that the success of legislation dealing with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> depends very much on the effectiveness of programs of this kind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* Both governmental and community based programs to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> are necessary. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* Under the Bill, the Commissioner will have the function of conducting and fostering programs of education and research to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, and a Community Relations Council will be established with an advisory role. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* Australia will be required by Article 7 of the Convention to conduct programs of this kind to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* It will provide the basis upon which Australia can comply with the obligations imposed by the Convention on Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The Bill is based on the view that laws proscribing <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> are vital, but not in themselves sufficient. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* The legislation recognises that there must also be effective and systematic enforcement of rights and the promotion of education and research if the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country is to be achieved in fact as well as in theory. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750415_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-43-0)

* We want to end all forms of sex <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750417_senate_29_s63/#debate-41)

* Will the Minister examine this matter and advise whether such practices would be in conflict with the proposed Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750422_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-5-0)

* The company claims that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is not involved but that it is a question of correct underwriting because nonwhite, non-Europeans have a lower life expectancy than Europeans. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750422_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-5-0)

* Section 13 of the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill which, I think, has reached the second reading stage in the Senate, provides - [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750422_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-5-0)

* I am sure this will be reflected in his attitude to the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill and other legislation which comes before the Senate. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750422_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-11-0)

* I can assure all honourable senators that the Australian Government insurance office will see that there will be no racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the provision of policies for any resident of this country who applies for them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750422_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-11-0)

* The essential quality of that is some balance and no <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, and certainly not preference. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750422_senate_29_s63/#debate-45)

* The Parliament may by any law with respect to trade or commerce forbid, as to railways, any preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by any State, or by any authority constituted under a State, if such preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State; due regard being had to the financial responsibilities incurred by any State in connection with the construction and maintenance of its railways. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750423_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-49-0)

* But no preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> shall, within the meaning of this section, be taken to be undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State, unless so adjudged by the InterState Commission. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750423_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-49-0)

* As it is International Women's Year, I wish to draw the attention of the Senate to various incidents which show how diligent a government must be and how difficult it is, until one actually has legislation to enforce an idea, to bring people to realise that they have a blind spot and that when it comes to matters such as <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> between the sexes, unfortunately, a deal of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> still exists. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750423_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-53-0)

* The matter that I wish to bring to the attention of the Senate concern <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against women. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750423_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-53-0)

* Again this is an example of how we can legislate against <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> but we have to take the ideas right through the community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750423_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-53-0)

* In this regard, of course, we have established <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> committees which are investigating these sorts of matters. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750423_senate_29_s63/#subdebate-53-0)

* Both administrations in South Vietnam, i.e., the PRG and the Saigon administration are to be treated without any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> whatsoever: either both will participate in the Conference or neither will. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750514_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-16-0)

* The other thing to do is to see that an office is established in Australia which will not function on the ground of race or sex <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-18-0)

* A racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill was first introduced in November 1973 and it was not presented to the Senate for debate prior to the Parliament being prorogued. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* A second racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill was introduced in April 1974 and that again was not presented to the Senate for debate. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* A third racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill was presented in October 1974 and that was withdrawn from the Senate in February 1975. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* On 15 April of this year this Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill was transmitted by message from the House of Representatives and today, after some 18 months, it comes before the Senate to be debated. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Opposition has many reservations about the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It recognises that the Bill gives expression to a desirable and acceptable principle- the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which proceeds from or which seeks to develop a superiority concept is to be deplored and avoided. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* A society which is plagued by the tensions of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is likely to be a society torn by dissension and evidencing a developing instability. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Bill of course ratifies the United Nations International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It seeks to establish its principles by providing, in general provisions, that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> shall be unlawful and by providing, through particular provisions, that certain types of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> shall be unlawful. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It is recognised by the Opposition that if we are to cope with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in a way that seeks to specify what are acts of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and to indicate a community disapproval of such conduct, then provisions of the character which are contained in the Bill are desirable. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Bill of course indicates- it is a provision to which we take exception- that if an act which could be regarded as an act of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> occurs and the reason for that act of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> occurring has a number of facets to it of which only one is the intention to do an act of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, then that is still to be regarded as an unlawful act. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* If an act of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> occurs it should be unlawful only if the dominant reason is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the grounds of racial or ethnic origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* If it be said that one reason why civil proceedings are not the appropriate proceedings under the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Act is because of the delicacy of the human relations which are involved, one might draw by way of comparison the fact that that has been the type of argument which has been used to justify certain types of proceedings before conciliation commissioners. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The first relates to the constitutional justification which might have been offered for this legislation; the second is to consider whether laws of this character can be expected to have the overall beneficial effects which can be claimed for legislation which deals with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>; and the third is to specify a little more precisely why the Opposition will propose its type of enforcement in preference to that which the Government has suggested. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* This is a Bill which seeks to make unlawful conduct which may be described broadly as conduct involving racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* There is no express power in the Constitution to make laws with respect to race relations or racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, or the conduct which may take place which is proscribed by this Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* What the Government is doing is relying upon the fact that there is an international convention for the elimination of all forms of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which Australia is ratifying and which, because of the obligations which it is said flow from that ratification, enables it to exercise its powers to make laws with respect to external affairs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* There also is an obligation upon a guarantor, a party to the convention, to declare as an offence punishable by law all dissemination of ideas based on racial superiority or hatred, or incitement to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as well as all acts of violence or incitement to such acts. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It shall declare illegal and prohibit organisations which promote and incite racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I object to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>; I object to communism, to fascism and to other forms of totalitarianism. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Notwithstanding that I object to communism, or fascism, or racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, I would recognise that it is the right of other people if they want to disseminate those views to be able to disseminate them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Convention proceeds, of course, on the basis that the propagation of any doctrine based on racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is scientifically false, is morally condemnable and socially unjust and that there is no justification for racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I think it has to be recognised today that there are few, if any, laws still remaining in this country which could be regarded as laws which involve a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It was said that the legislation has a vital role to play in the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The proscribing of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in legislative form will make people more aware of the evils of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and will make it more obvious and conspicuous. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It may be that that will be a consequence of the Bill, but whether that will aid in the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is very much open to question, because the more there is a concentration and a focusing of attention on an issue which to many people has never been an issue at all, the more it will create problems which never before were problems. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The fact that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is unlawful will make it easier for people to resist social pressures that result in <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I think that people desire to observe the law, and if they know it is unlawful to engage in acts of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> then I think there will be a tendency and a willingness to accept that that is a conformity which they must respect. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I know that in the United Kingdom where the racial tensions have a far greater recognition than in Australia there has been legislation designed to avoid racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> since, I think, 1966. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* If one looks at the commentaries in the news reports, one realises that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is as great and as much a source of friction in the United Kingdom today as it ever was. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The effectiveness of the Act has been particularly marked in virtually removing discriminatory notices and advertisements from shop windows and newspapers and there are strong reasons to believe that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in services and places of public resort has greatly diminished. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* On the other hand, although it appears that the Act has had beneficial effects in the fields of unemployment and housing the board considers that there is still evidence of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, especially in promotion opportunities and the 'white collar' sector of employment and in private housing. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The other publication to which I refer is 'The Extent of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The results of our tests demonstrate that there is still substantial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against members of the minority groups when seeking jobs and housing. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* They also show that this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is more related to race than to foreign origin, since the level of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against Italians or Greeks is comparatively low. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Although the level of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> seems, therefore, to be lower now than it was before the Act, the general conclusion from these findings must be that the number of cases of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that are dealt with by the law (either by means of conciliation or by means of legal sanctions) forms a very small proportion of the number of acts of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that actually occur. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* We in Australia have been singularly free of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* That is the concept in this Bill-  which is inherent in the International Convention on the Elimination of all forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> becomes continually more and more plainly correct and it will be a notable day when this country of ours can join those who have ratified the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Senator Greenwood  said also that this Bill would declare illegal organisations which foster racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* There is a great need to declare illegal those organisations which foster racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The reasons for <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> have never been terribly important. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* What is important is that there is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* There is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on any number of grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* There is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because of sex, age, race, colour, religious or political beliefs, an accident of birth, or otherwise. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Senator Greenwood  spoke of the previous racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)
