* Everyone is entitled without any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to the equal protection of the law. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Honourable senators will be aware, of course, that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against women is nothing new in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Women have traditionally met <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> when they have endeavoured to obtain finance, particular for housing and major purchases. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* When looking at <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> we must take in the situation which existed in Western Australia until at least 12 months ago when it was not even possible because of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> for a woman to sign a guarantee for her son or daughter to continue his or her tertiary education. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* If we are looking at <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against women in general we cannot bypass what happens in the Parliament. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I remind  Senator Wright,  who is trying to interject, that Aboriginal women are included in the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that we are specifically looking at today is just as apparent in many other areas. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* We have all read reports of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, and some of us have been fortunate enough, or unfortunate enough, to see instances of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* 
 Senator Greenwood mentioned earlier that the Convention would declare illegal organisations which foster racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I think honourable senators should give a few moments thought to the background of the matter before the Senate, which is the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* -We are discussing the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill 1975 but after hearing that speech by  Senator Coleman  we could be forgiven for falling into some confusion because for all we know it could have been a discussion on a Bill on <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the grounds of sex, income level, drugs, family power- anything but racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Problems of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> do not occur in the socialist countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Those countries are not subject to the same problems in racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as we are here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Because of these problems, once again created by governments, we are now faced with this Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* In my opinion if this Bill is implemented it will create more <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, not less. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* This Bill is being brought in on the grounds that Australia is a party to the International Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The introduction of the Bill is supported by the Schedule of the International Con vention on the Elimination of All Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>, and claims that the charter of the United Nations is based on the dignity and equality inherent in all human beings. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Far from eliminating racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by making it illegal, the Bill will highlight the problems between the races and create an official race relations industry with a staff of dedicated anti-racists earning their living by making the most of every complaint in much the same way as does the Race Relations Board in the United Kingdom. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It is somewhat incongruous that we find the Opposition parties criticising this Government which outlined in its policy speech- it also is in the program of the Australian Labor Party- its determination to play a significant part in abolishing any forms of racial, political and economic <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I find racism the most objectionable and most obnoxious form of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I cannot understand how any Australian, or for that matter, any person can ever defend the sort of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that has taken place in this country and many other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Bill sets out very simply to ratify an international convention to make it unlawful for any person to practice racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* This Government is seeking to introduce legislation designed to meet Australia's obligations under the international convention on the elimination of all forms of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I can quote no better authority on the question of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> than the founder of the Australian Liberal Party,  Sir Robert  Menzies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Nobody can disagree, surely, with the proposition that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> continues to flourish in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* My colleague,  Senator Coleman,  has given abundant evidence that this form of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> exists very far and very wide in our country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* What is required are strong, operable, measures designed to eliminate racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in order that a more free and equal Australian society can emerge from the scourge of prejudice. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It recognises also that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> cannot be curbed solely by legal means. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I am grateful for the small mercy that at least  Mr W.  C. Wentworth in another place said that he would support that portion of the legislation which seeks to implement the Convention and to carry out a program of education in order that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is no longer fostered in our community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* On the third front against racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> the Bill provides for the settlement of alleged racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by non-legal means. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Senator Sheil,  who preceded me in the debate, seemed to think that if some responsibility were passed on to an eminent person within the community to examine and regulate these problems of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> it would result in the setting up some form of bureaucracy and that that should be avoided at all costs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* According to the legislation, every endeavour is to be made by the Commissioner to settle the matter, to promote understanding, to deal with the lesser excesses of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in a non-legal manner. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I witnessed racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The role of education in eradicating social <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> cannot be over-emphasised, and the Bill does precisely that. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The role can be made more meaningful and effective if expressions and actions of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> are prohibited. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Without this legal sanction the Bill would have little effect in curbing racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* The Bill would be nothing more than an empty declaration of good intent or a belated recognition that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> exists in our country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* No one could assert that there is no racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* That fact ought to be a constant reminder to us of what happens when people advocate armchair fashion attitudes and policies against <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and do nothing. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Who thinks that words are stronger than deeds- those who deny the existence of racism, those who talk about prejudice as if it does not exist, those who say this legislation ought not to be carried and those who are concerned to protect the guilty rather than the innocent victims of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* If a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill ought to have been in operation at any time it was at the time that the Tasmanian Aborigines were being exterminated by the settlers in that State. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> against the Aborigine in the administration of the criminal law and in the enjoyment of civil, political and technical rights still exists. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* In the past 180 years Aborigines have suffered enormous handicaps in Australian society by comparison with whites, commencing with violent dispossession of their land and destruction of their social fabric, and continuing through various forms of legal, social and economic <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* Many of the existing practices of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> will be outlawed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It will become possible now for those public officials to be charged with <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> if they persist in their unfair and discriminatory practices which are synoymous with the activities of certain policemen in the Redfern area, activities have been noted by lawyers of substance in the region, activities which are continuing to this very day to the everlasting disgrace of sections of the New South Wales police force. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* One would imagine, when one listens to the Opposition, that we have never had a problem associated with racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* We opened our hearts, we brought them here and then we began a policy of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* We have had the opportunity in the last few days to examine the forms of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> practised against the migrant population in our country by the insurance companies, those great citadels of capital accumulation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* I never realised until I was elected to this place the degree of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to which the previous LiberalCountry Party Government turned a blind eye for so many years. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It took no steps to eradicate these forms of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It was not until the United Nations and other international organisations drew the attention of the Australian Government to these forms of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that we had an opportunity to compensate these people for the forms of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which have been practised. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* This is one of the companies that have the temerity to challenge the established and declared policy as enunciated in the policy speech of the Prime Minister  (Mr Whitlam)  on 2 occasions that we shall establish an Australian Government Insurance Office in which there shall be no <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on sex, race or religion. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* One has only to look at the propaganda from the Rights Committee that operates in the far north coast area of New South Wales and in Queensland to see that that organisation makes racism and <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> a cornerstone of its policies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It is the subtle unspoken <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which has to be eradicated. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* An unspoken inhuman <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>- which I am sure was the substance of the behaviour of the insurance companies and of many others- from time to time manifests itself in a racist comment or joke and maintains the alienation felt by the migrant and the Aboriginal from the so-called original Australians. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* We write to urge your support of the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* It was moved and seconded That this general Meeting of the Australian Council of Churches supports the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill, 1974, and informs the AttorneyGeneral of this, at the same time requesting him to ensure that those minority groups which suffer from dis.crirnination have substantial representation on the Community Relations Council which will be set up if the Bill is enacted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-45-0)

* To my mind the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill 1975 that is before us is, in its present form, in many aspects of the over-government type and is restrictive of the freedom of Australian citizens to express their opinions freely and to conduct their own affairs in accordance with the dictates of their consciences. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>' is a term which should be used very carefully. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Personally, I define 'racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>' as an expression of malice towards any human being because of his race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Therefore, I have no personal difficulty in agreeing fully with the assertion that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is evil. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I am not so sure that coercive measures will help to combat prejudice and <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* There is a vitally important area of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which, I feel, could cause more harm, hurt and damage than many other forms of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I believe that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the sense of making or constituting a difference in or between people is morally wrong in whatever way it comes about. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* However, as soon as we want to combat <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the basis of race, colour, descent, national or ethnic origin and class, we should adhere to the great tradition of this country that a person is innocent unless proven guilty. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Therefore in my opinion any racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill should include a reference to the immoral ideologies by which racism is promoted at the expense of the dignity of humanity and all its individual members. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I trust that as a result of certain amendments being carried this legislation will finally emerge as good, effective and just legislation and legislation that is actually able to achieve, in a way in which the Australian people would desire it, the elimination of whatever <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is present in our country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* -The Senate is debating the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Senator Laucke,  who preceded me in the debate, confused me with some of the attitudes he took towards the Bill, particularly that which he expressed as a desire to abolish class <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* The first of those basic principles is that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> should be proscribed by law and that fundamental rights should be guaranteed without distinction as to race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* So the outlawing of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by legal sanctions is also a basis for changing community standards. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* As a fourth principle the Bill emphasises the importance of the use of education and other programs to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I have said 'helping to solve this problem in Australia' because nobody on this side of the House would pretend for one moment that by passing a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill we are in any way solving the problem of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I think that the highest we can seriously put it is that we believe- of course, we gather that the Opposition also believes- that the passing of this legislation will assist and facilitate the lessening of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* While that is true, the origins of the Bill can be found perhaps in the United Nations Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> which was signed by Australia in 1966. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Since 1966 nothing very much happened in this country in relation to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> until this legislation was introduced. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* It is an interesting fact and a very happy fact for this country that both major political parties have in their platforms clauses which specifically deplore racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* In 1971 the Australian United Nations Association set up in Australia a committee to combat racism and racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* That committee, which had the support and co-operation of all the major churches in Australia, most major welfare organisations and both major political parties, made representations to State and Commonwealth governments asking them to introduce legislation prohibiting <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the grounds of race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* When I was going around in nappies there was a lot of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country and there still is. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* The lady in question took great pains to describe the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill as rubbish, and she used other terminology of a similar kind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* This group says that under the Commonwealth Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill and Human Rights Bill and the Victorian Avoidance of <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill a person who chooses to marry his or her race, ethnic group, nationality, or religion, and not to marry a person of another race, ethnic group, nationality or religion, does an act involving a distinction, exclusion, restriction or preference based on colour, descent, national or ethnic origin or religion can be prosecuted and could happen under the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* As I understand it, what this group is saying is that according to the view which it is spreading about the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill a person who makes a choice to marry a person of Australian ethnic origin can be prosecuted because that is racially discriminatory, but of course that is just stupid and it is typical of the sort of thing which is printed in this type of publication I referred to earlier. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I want to refer to one other example of this sort of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in our society. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* One English migrant wrote to a newspaper about the British anti-<span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill and indicated the great disturbance and divisions it had caused in that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I have not found any great <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against people like that. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Can we be accused of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because a particular person goes to morning tea with me or somebody else goes with another person to morning tea or afternoon tea, or to supper or to have their meals? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Can that be said to be <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* When we are talking about <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, the term can have a very wide aspect. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* The honourable senator is a legal man; so I ask him where this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> ends. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I exonerate  Senator Button  from such remarks because he did have the good sense to say that apart from one or two speeches this really has not been a debate on an anti-<span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill but it has been more like a debate on a migration Bill. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* We have been speaking of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and racism but let us consider where this exists. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* We in Australia are just amateurs in racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* Is that not racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750515_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* If it appears to the Minister that the Commission is showing undue preference to, or is exercising undue <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against, any person or persons of any 'class or description in the charges or other terms or conditions applicable to services provided by it, he may, after consultation with the Commission, give it such directions as appear to him requisite to secure that it ceases so to do. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750520_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-42-0)

* If it appears to the Minister that the Commission is showing undue preference to, or is exercising undue <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against, any person or persons of any class or description in the charges or other terms or conditions applicable to services provided by it, he may, after consultation with the Commission, give it such directions as appear to him requisite to secure that it ceases so to do. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750520_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-42-0)

* Section 102 of the Constitution provides that the Parliament may make laws forbidding undue or unreasonable preference on <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by state railway systems. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* A State, or an authority of a State, shall not, as to any railway, in respect of or so as to affect trade or commerce among the States, give any preference or make any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that the Commission has adjudged undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* He said that it was necessary to clothe the Commission with sufficient power to deal with railway rates, <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, rebates and all other forms of unfair treatment, as has been done in the United States of America where they have established a United States Commerce Commission. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* I do not lapse into legalism, but the point I wish to make is that the purpose of the InterState Commission, as it was envisaged by the framers of the Constitution was that it was designed to deal with problems which arose from <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> so far as valid laws were concerned. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* All it can do is act in relation to preferences and <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> under valid laws. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* For example, if one examines clause 10 one finds that the Parliament is arrogating to itself a power to declare unlawful, in respect of or so as to affect overseas transport or interstate transport or in relation to overseas transport or interstate transport, any preference or advantage, <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> or disadvantage which the Commissioner adjudges to be undue and unreasonable. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* What if the InterState Commission was to declare some charges to be unreasonable or to be a <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750521_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-46-0)

* -Has the Minister for Manufacturing Industry seen Press reports of a speech by the Queensland  President  of the Institute of Surveyors,  Mr K.  Davies, to the effect that there is confusion and demoralisation in Australia's small business sector and that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against small enterprises is rife in Australia? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-23-0)

* The Government also recognises that there is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against small firms. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-23-0)

* To help counter this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> we initiated measures in the Trade Practices Act to prohibit price <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-23-0)

* It is a fact that there is this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> law in Queensland. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-27-0)

* I am sure that the legislation on our notice paper- the Bill that has been through the Senate and the House of Representatives and now has been returned to the Senate with some proposed amendments- will overcome the <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that now applies to Aborigines on settlements in Queensland. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-27-0)

* The Parliament may by any law with respect to trade or commerce forbid, as to railways, any preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> by any State, or by any authority constituted under a State, if such preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State; due regard being had to the financial responsibilities incurred by any State in connexion with the construction and maintenance of its railways. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-39-0)

* But no preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> shall, within the meaning of this section, be taken to be undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State, unless so adjudged by the Inter-State Commission. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-39-0)

* subject any particular person, State, locality or class or kind of transport to any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> or disadvantage, that the Commission has adjudged to be undue and unreasonable. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-39-0)

* 1 ) A State, or an authority of a State, shall not, as to any railway, in respect of or so as to affect trade or commerce among the States, give any preference or make any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that the Commission has adjudged undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-39-0)

* In deciding whether the doing of any act or thing constitutes for the purposes of sub-section ( 1 ) a preference or <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that is undue and unreasonable, or unjust to any State, the Commission shall have due regard to the financial responsibilities incurred by any State in connection with the construction and maintenance of its railways. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-39-0)

* -Some days ago this matter was before the Senate for debate and I spoke for some time then on this Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill, so let me give a quick resume. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* What is racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Is it <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because of the different nationalities of people? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Is it <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because of the different colour of people? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Is it <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because some people are not as well off as are others, or because of whatever other aspect we may think of? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Therefore, the matter of accepting one another, getting on well with one another, and of not having <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> depends in many cases upon individuals. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Are we to be accused of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> because we do not like those people? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is a case of personal desires and personal likes, but legislation such as this Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill when put into effect, is the type of thing that can cause to develop, in the minds of certain people in this country, an attitude on racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that can be of a very dangerous character. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is easy to say, 'Someone acted against me racially', or That person showed racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Jewish people have achieved a greatness, a development and an enrichment in many ways because they did not allow this silly business of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to worry them and to beat them down. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am not saying that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is good. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I have not seen any <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I realise that it is often most difficult to establish <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on race, colour or ethnic grounds, and of course there is always the risk of creating the converse situation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is nothing worse than the mental cruelty that can be and is being inflicted on minority groups in our community by so-called law abiding citizens, and when the only ground for this <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is racial it is indeed high time that something was done about that form of cruelty which not only disadvantages a person in the fields of employment and housing but robs him of his dignity and his pride. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* This Bill helps to protect people from racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the fields of employment and housing and in access to places and facilities. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* However, I will say that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the 1970s is not as blatant as it was in the 1950s, but it is just as latent, and that is where the danger lies- in the latent <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that goes on, especially in our education system. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am talking about people in ethnic groups who protect themselves from being disappointed or hurt simply by not applying for higher employment or better accommodation, solely because of the fear of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on sheer racial grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Parties, for example, to the International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> undertake to adopt immediate and effective measures, particularly in the fields of teaching, education, culture and information with a view to combating prejudices which tend to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and to promoting understanding and tolerance'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* That the widest possible educational and publicity campaign be undertaken and, in particular among disadvantaged sections of the population, with respect to the Human Rights Bill and the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill, if and when enacted, and the Legal Aid Schemes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Because we live in a materialistic society today rather than a religious society, the same urge exists to solve all the problems of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> of one sort of another, not by the canonical law but by statute of Parliament. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* She attacked the whole problem of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the basis of sexualism that is to say, women are a deprived element in the community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against women as a sexual problem will not be remedied by passing laws. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I turn to what I regard as the most dreadful form of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which came out inferentially in  Senator Button's  speech. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* As  Senator Sheil  has said, the problems in relation to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia exist to a large degree because we have tried to create a multiracial society at least based on some common ground of a European descent, which  Senator Mcintosh  appears to disregard. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I accept the declaration by the United Nations Organisation that there should be no <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the terms in which the United Nations made this declaration. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The propaganda which was distributed in Australia by the United Nations Organisation and which was mentioned by  Senator Mcintosh  states that the United Nations was unanimous on this declaration regarding racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>; that all the people in the United Nations subscribe to this declaration without any demurrer. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I have here a list of the nations that have acceded to the United Nations International Convention for the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There it is, a great part of the sub-continent of Asia with some 450 million or 500 million people, wracked by racial, religious and caste discriminations, yet that country acceded to the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Government of India declared that for reference of any dispute in the International Court of Justice, for decision in terms of article 22 of the International Convention for the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>, the consent of all parties to the dispute is necessary in each individual case. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Finally, the United States throws the whole Convention out of the window and says: 'We will make our own arrangements in relation to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the grounds of religion, cast and colour'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* We give the ground away, not on the basis that we are ashamed in any way, but simply on the argument that I first adduced, namely, that you cannot eliminate <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the ground of religion, race, colour or anything else except if it is done by an educated society. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If honourable senators have read the Melbourne 'Herald' this week they would know that in the Canadian Province of Ontario, which  Senator Button  praised as having a model statute of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> of one sort or another, there is more <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> than in any of the other Canadian Provinces. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Yet it has this model racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> legislation which, as I mentioned earlier, carries this exception to protect  Senator Coleman  from affronts of one sort and another. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Observations were made by  Senator Gietzelt  about racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in the election which  Mr Grassby  lost. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In 18 cases, it was decided that there had been  <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Twenty-two complaints in the sale of houses were investigated and <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> found in 3 cases . [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Race Relations Act seems to have been effective in reducing <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in public houses. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The population of the United Kingdom is involved in racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to an infinitely more emphatic degree than the population of this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Race Relations Board and its committees found 23 cases of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> concerning public houses in 1970-71 and in twenty-two of those cases conciliation was successful. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* All I am saying is that there is racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The report of the select committee of the House of Commons in Great Britain- it is the third of such reports- found that the causes of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> were other than colour, caste and creed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It will not solve the problem of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as referred to in the United Nations Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* First of all it must tackle the problem of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> at its base. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> problem in which he is involved. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Work in it will probably begin to solve the problem of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Because we are committed internationally to try to solve this problem, I believe we must introduce a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> statute onto the Australian statute books. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Notwithstanding the comments of  Senator Sir Magnus  Cormack and the references that he made to  Senator Button  and 1 or 2 other colleagues of mine, I do not believe that anyone on this side of the chamber believes that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> can be entirely legislated out of existence. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The fact that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is unlawful will make it easier for people to resist social pressures that result in <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Having been born and reared in a country town which like most country towns in Australia manifested quite a deal of anti-Aboriginal <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, I have seen examples of the relevance of the point that  Senator James  McClelland was making. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The barber states in a town where racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> does exist that if he cuts the Aboriginal's hair his European customers will not patronise his shop; they will go somewhere else. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If on the other hand the barber is in a position to say 'the law forbids me from discriminating against Aboriginals' he is then in a very much stronger position to resist those very social pressures for racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> to which  Senator James  McClelland referred. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The Bill prohibits racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and incitment to racial hatred. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* However,  Senator Greenwood  did not bother to mention that the laws of defamation already provide substantial constraints against an absolute freedom of expression and of publication, nor did he explain why if the Bill is objectionable on those grounds the Government of which he was a member in 1966 voted for the United Nations Convention on Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> which is appended to this Bill and which provides for exactly the same prohibitions against incitement to racial hatred and the publication or dissemination of racist propaganda. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He then proceeded to tell us that in terms of racial persecution and racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> we in Australia were just amateurs and that we had a lot to learn from the natives. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I rise to welcome the presentation of this Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill to this chamber and to congratulate the Government for having introduced it into the Parliament. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> document which the United Nations produced was executed by the previous Government in 1 966. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is my view that it is a pity that following the execution of that document legislation was not enacted at a State level, where there is less constitutional uncertainty, to deal with the question of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In other words, 1 am seeking to assert the thesis that it is the view of this entire Parliament that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, one of the disfigurements of the 20th century, should be silenced. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is some difference of opinion about the machinery that ought to be utilised by society and by government to bring an end to racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I think there is nothing improper or disgraceful about having differences of opinion about the machinery, but I stress the unanimity of the Parliament in condemning racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I say to the Minister in charge of the Bill that he ought to give very careful consideration to the amendments which will be put forward by the Opposition in the Committee stage of this Bill, because it is certainly my conviction that the amendments will in fact improve the legislation, would enable it to be introduced far more successfully into the community, and would in the long term aid the objective which I am sure the Government has of reducing racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The second important fact is that there is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I have listened to my fortunate colleagues who have spent time overseas tell us that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in other countries is worse than it is here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Since I do not have the benefit of that experience, I cannot say whether they are right or wrong, but I can say that my own experience tells me that <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in this country is at a level which I find totally unacceptable. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* When I speak of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> I simply mean that a large number of people are treated not because of what they are but because of their racial heritage- because their parents were Aboriginal, Greek, or of some other race. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In my professional life I came across a consistent series of examples of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> on the grounds of race that I found highly objectionable, and on many occasions the law did not provide an adequate remedy. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* That, to me, is blatant <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, and this woman was subjected to it not only by a government department but also by my own profession. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* This platform, which was adopted only last year, provides on page 17 that 'the maintenance of individual freedom calls for positive measures by the Government and private organisations to encourage equal opportunity and to prevent <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against the individual or minority groups'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I agree with many honourable senators who have pointed out that to legislate against <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is extremely difficult. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In just the same way, if we have a legislative framework which declares that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is illegal, that legislative framework in itself has some educative effect and it is part of the environment and the context in which people grow up. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I do think that law has a place in moulding community attitudes and that therefore the declaration that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia should be illegal is useful in itself as a long term educative tool. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Quite apart from that, of course, the Bill, even if it cannot change attitudes immediately, can prevent overt acts of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which are harmful to individuals. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* His  article carries the heading 'The Role of Legislation in Eliminating Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I have had some experience of matters which have been drawn to the attention of the Minister for Aboriginal Affairs  (Senator Cavanagh)  over the past year or two in which, in my judgment as a lawyer who has had some practise in this field, it would be difficult to obtain solutions simply by going to the courts because quite often people who are the subject of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> are the sort of people who are least able to take advantage of court procedures. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In my view, the important thing is that the people of Australia should see that a Bill comes out of this Parliament that has the unanimous support of the Parliament, because I think that that in itself will be a big propaganda victoryand I use the word 'propaganda' in a nonoffensive sense, I hope- for those people who believe that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> should be destroyed in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If those people who are actively discriminating on the ground of race see that the whole of the Parliament is united in this declaration that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> should be unlawful, I believe some will lose heart at least to some extent and cease the sort of campaign that I think has been offensive to most of us. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* Those people I have an obligation to look after under my portfolio have been referred to frequently and I think it would be accepted that, if there was any racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia, they would be the most aggrieved people by any racist attitude of the Australia public or of any sections of our community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If it is established that discriminatory action was taken because an ethnic group was involved, then there is an offence and, as  Senator Walsh  said, it establishes social support for the individual to refrain from using <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There are some people who may say that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> acts in 2 ways and that some preference is being given to Aborigines at the present time by way of the allocation of funds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is significant that a Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill has only now reached the Senate after having been first introduced in November 1973. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* In my opinion, Australia is not in the throes of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>; and I emphasise that. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He said that there is a pocket of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>; he said it is a pocket of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am not prepared to admit that there is that pocket of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is a pocket of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, and there is a difference between normal <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I say that Australia is not in the throes of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> for these reasons: Accepted Government policy has decreed that Australia is not in the throes of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* So we do not have that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> of which we have heard so much tonight. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There will be isolated cases, but on an overall basis we do not have racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in our area. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* But because of that isolated pocket of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> referred to by  Senator Cavanagh,  we have presented to us legislation which in my humble opinion is going to be very difficult to implement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I am not aware of blatant racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, but I am fully aware of many acts of <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> galore in this chamber. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against people because of their likes and dislikes for music, the arts and everything else that one could imagine. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against men who wear their hair long. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* There is <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> all along the line. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* A person could think: 'I did not get this employment because of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>'. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* If there were racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> I would do my best, not only as a legislator but as a person, to see that it was stopped. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is not fair that there should be racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* I honestly think that this legislation could be the means of insulting that section of the new races we have in Australia because it implies racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in an area in which I think it does not exist. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* He did not say that there was racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* So we have a state of affairs today in which people who have played a part in our society will get the idea that there is racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* It is a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> of which 99 per cent of our community are not aware. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* We must ask ourselves this question: Has racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in Australia reached a point at which legislation is necessary? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750522_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-44-0)

* The book implies that there have been blatant examples of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> against a trained Aboriginal nursing sister who is employed by the Aboriginal Medical Service in Sydney. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-12-0)

* They show the existence of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-12-0)

* It is apparent from them that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is in fact occurring. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-12-0)

* Just before the close of business last Thursday evening the Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill came before the Senate and I spent 2 minutes speaking by way of introduction. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill comes to the Senate at this hour of the evening by way of contrast. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Matters of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, matters of social equality and indeed matters of social inequality are very important and in current conversation have become popular issues today. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span> Bill implements into our Australian law the obligations that are contained in the International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In short, the Bill now before the Senate seeks to make racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unlawful. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I use the term 'racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>' in the sense in which I read it in the United Nations Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The Bill makes it unlawful for a person to do an act- I am looking very broadly at the Schedule which is contained in the Bill- involving <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> based on race, colour, descent and national or ethnic origin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* These procedures are related to complaints of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* There is an aspect of the Bill which relates to the development of programs of education and research which are designed to combat racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The United Nations International Convention on the Elimination of all Forms of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>- this is the area, as every honourable senator knows, to which this legislation is related- evolved after a good deal of study and analysis of the very difficult and sensitive matter of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> around the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* After all, any discussion, study or research into the whole area of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> involves human relations, a whole lot of economic conditions and a whole lot of international conditions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* As most honourable senators know, a declaration on the elimination of all forms of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> was drafted and was adopted in 1963. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In general terms the Convention condemns and seeks the elimination of all forms of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The term 'racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>' is one on which we can have debate and discussion over a long period of time but I take it at this point of speaking to the Senate in this debate to mean, as it was quoted in the Convention: [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* It is true to say that the Convention provides for us comprehensive measures of implementation and there is also the Committee on the Elimination of Racial <span class="highlight">Discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This Committee has been established to receive reports on the existence of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> and to implement methods of conciliation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* While we may have some support for the thrust of the Bill and the principles which it puts forward, legislation alone does not solve the problem of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>, the problem of relationships between person and person. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* If I recall his words correctly, he made reference to the fact that legislation has only a role to play in the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The Minister said the Bill is a step towards the objective as outlined in the Bill, so the Government has put down a measure which, while it is very comprehensive, is conceded by the Minister in presenting it to the Senate as having only a role to play and is a step towards the elimination of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* In any program for the abolition of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which involves the well being of a total community, a state or a nation the community must be reminded over and over again that it has a role and there are steps that it must take and that it has involvement and a responsibility in such a program. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* This is referred to in various clauses of the Bill, and it relates to the dissemination of ideas on racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> as contained in article 4. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I think that in any discussion on racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> it is important that nations involved take unto themelves the high responsibility of legislating as far as domestic matters are concerned. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* There is no doubt in my mind that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> is something that we should seek to eliminate by the most effective means possible. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* After all, as I said earlier, it is comparatively easy to lay down legislative processes that would seek to eliminate racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> but when you come to implementing them in human terms I ask the question: How do we really do it, do it effectively, and how do we do it so that the total society benefits and so that relations between persons and person, group and group, and community and community are maintained for the benefit and total development of the whole? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I suppose it is easy to say that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> exists right round the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* While I might say that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> has existed throughout history that does not excuse me from being involved in legislative processes, or any other processes, that may help to avoid <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* The fact is that mankind has had to wrestle, at some level almost throughout history, with the fact that racial and other discriminations have existed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Because we might exist in a majority group and because we have got into the habit of stereotyping other groups, believe it or not we develop into a situation whereby <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> unfortunately thrives. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* We of a European society and tradition are concerned about racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* It is not without importance to observe that racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> has been a factor not only of European society, it also has been a factor of other societies, and references have been made in this debate to <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> in other communities. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Because <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> exists in other communities, that does not give us any justification whatever for allowing it to continue and exist in our own. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Most ethnic <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> that we see in Australia is related to differences which occur as a result of the circumstances which have developed, particularly in the last 50 to 100 years. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I guess we could have some debate and argument on all of these things, but the fact is that some <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> has been developing within our Australian society. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I think it probably is true to say that we have been spared the worst excesses of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> simply because of the other conditions that developed in our society at the time that there were discriminating references and habits. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I make this reference because I think it is important in a discussion on a racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> Bill but I do not speak for the Committee and therefore my references must be general and I must speak purely from personal observation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* Allegations of racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> within our Australian society have been many in the experiences I have had in relation to that Committee, but I would not be prepared to stand up and prove them in this Senate because there is a whole range of other circumstances related to such incidents. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* But I have been greatly concerned as I have gone around and heard evidence of the existence of what appears to me to be <span class="highlight">discrimination</span> which is unfortunate and hurtful to the people concerned. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)

* I may be wrong in describing this as racial <span class="highlight">discrimination</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/senate/1975/19750527_senate_29_s64/#subdebate-54-0)
